First time coming here for lunch after seeing the line outside for the longest time I had to go try it out for myself. I got the Kung Pow Chicken with steamed rice which I thought was a comfrtable spicy. Best Chinese place in SL I've been to so far, it definitly wasn't like some other chinese resteraunts that just overload the oil and the flavor. But this place seems pretty authentic. Nice workers also, they work hard to make the food for all the people getting coming for lunch and dinner<//review>

<user>109581647313759883609<//user><name>Kristina Long<//name><time>1513351406127<//time><rate>4</rate>< text>
Lots of open green grassy space, sports fields, fun play structure equipment fir both tiny tots and older children as well. Plenty of sun, with plenty of shady spots to escape the heat and there's usually a cool breeze in the later afternoons. There's a few benches for us grown ones to watch over and read or secretly play games on our phones, also a few tables and benches for picnics and BBQs...and yes, there are public bathrooms available but I'm fairly certain they're only unlocked during daylight hours.  It is adjacent to Pine Valley Middle school, however I do not believe that they use the heart of the park for recess.< /text>

< Review>
This place was packed when we got there. I was surprised as we are going through a pandemic. The restaurant looked to it's full capacity.
The food was okay nothing special. We ordered some appetizers fish tacos and a combination plate.
The decor was also okay.
The staff, however, did an EXCELLENT job!  The lady at the front putting people on the waitlist was very friendly and attended to us right away. Our waiter was also amazing. He was very knowledgeable, helpful, and attentive.
So what they fall short in in other things, they make up for in their staff. I would come back just because of the service.
The live music, although you had to pay for it, was also really great!<//Review>

I'm sorry but I have to leave a review this time. I have been to this place many times. I didn't like it the first time so I gave  it a second chance and the outcome was the same. < Review>
UPDATE 5/25/2019:

I need to update my review of Murrieta's for one simple reason.  The food is great but service is less then perfect sometimes. On this day my wife and I decided to go to Murrieta's for a late lunch. We were in a hurry because we had some appointments that we had to keep. When we arrived the restaurant was not full as you would expect (it was probably at 20 or 30% capacity). We were promptly seated and served our food that we really enjoyed, but soon after we finished eating our server didn't come back as you would expect. We only wanted our bill to pay and go quickly because of our appointments. We asked another person that was serving drinks and were ignored. After a long time I got up to the front of the restaurant and there was nobody there. It was until I asked the camera guy about paying that he pointed me to a server (Different than our original). while we waited up front  this other server finally gave me my check but it was the wrong one and had to wait a bit longer to get the right one. Finally paid and got out of there and were late for our appointment. I have been here when the restaurant is super busy and delays like this are expected but not when the restaurant is more than half empty. Hope that management reads this and improves on service. Food greatness is not the only thing that makes a restaurant excellent, service is in my opinion the same or more important.

Hopefully Murrietas's can go back to 5 stars after future visits.

-------------------------------------------
OLDER REVIEW:

Last time I was here my son was a baby and now he is 19. My wife and I ordered ceviche and pollo en mole and I can say  both items were very good . More the mole than the ceviche. The place was packed. We will be back sooner<//Review>

< review>
I was taken to Murrieta's Mexican Restaurant by two close friends of mine and I thought that it was one of the best Mexican restaurants that I have eaten at in the whole County of San Diego.
The inside was made up of myriad different types of polished wood with all kinds of Mexican styles of artwork...just really classic. There were the old style leather booths and plants everywhere. The din of the lights and light Spanish music made Murrieta's a great place to relax and enjoy a menu with many orderves and some uniquely Mexican food ; you can get lost in the number of menu choices.
I had a cheese enchilada and a beef enchilada and it was delicious. My two friends had different dishes that are quite popular.
We had lemon and strawberry margaritas-the kind with salt around the lip of the glasses- which were really good.
Their chips were unique because each one was quite thin, instead of the typical thick "tooth crackers." In fact, it would be nice if more restaurants and manufacturers made their chips like Murrieta's. They were also were served with a bowl of thick red sauce ( The chips and bowls of red sauce come with the meals; they also have green sauce).
I suggest that you try this restaurant for yourself if you or you and your friends want some of the best Mexican food in town.
I could say a lot more but, I highly recommend that you seek out this restaurant for yourselves. and you be glad that you did!
It's a great place to relax and get away from this fast paced world and is located near the Bonita area.< /review>

The food was great. I got flautas, which I hadn't had before, and they were very soft and tasted great. The beans, rice, chips and guacamole all seemed to be made fresh in house, along with the flour tortillas that came with the heaping steak fajitas. <rate>4</rate>< Review>
The food is okay, though I don't think the menu has changed in decades. Standard Californian-Mexican.

The wait staff is friendly and efficient. The outdoor seating is nice most of the year.

This seems to be the local place people most go to for celebratory meals, and it's great for that.

You might have to wait 20 minutes or so at peak times unless you have a reservation.

A few vegetarian dishes are available.

There's a separate bar on the southern end. Occasionally you might see a horse waiting outside. No spittoons or  grizzled, world-weary sheriffs, though.<//Review>

< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< text>
This is an honest review from a former restaurant owner. The reason for this being a 4 star review is that in my opinion it is not a 5 star restaurant. There are no James Beard award winning chefs here and they have no nouveau creative inspirations anywhere on the menu. What they DO have is a warm welcoming authentic MEXICAN restaurant. The kind I grew up in, and the kind that should never die. The flavors of all their sauces shows that they take the time to do it right, and they pass my test for a rating a 4/5 star on my scale. That test you may ask? Beans and rice. The beans are great and the rice is ehhh. As any chef of Mexican food will tell you, beans and rice both take a lot of time to get right. However the best Spanish rice requires a lot of attention and beans do their own thing over time. Most restaurant kitchens are far too busy, but if they can still nail the rice and sauces they get a 5 from me. I'll be back.</text>

<pictures>None<//pictures><GmapID>0x80d95025865b75d1:0x23d595cbf08b554c< /GmapID>< Review>
This is a Mexican food restaurant that has been around for 30+ years. The atmosphere is traditional Mexican; the food is excellent; & the service is good. I think it is the best Mexican food place to eat in Bonita. Great prices and large portions of food. The chips are freshly made. Don't eat too many chips & salsa before your meal comes out...you will not have room in your stomach left. Excellent place to take family & friends from out of town that want authentic Mexican food!</Review>

Nice crispy fries for the kids, chips salted while warm so it sticks, and no hitches. This last time we brought family visiting and I raved about the place then the queso dip came way too oily, the fries were baked and reheated so the kids wouldn't even eat them, plain chips, and the same corn I have ordered before was now not sweet and clearly dumped straight from a can. <Review>So for Father's Day my daughter wanted to take me out for dinner.  Knowing that our regular place to eat out was packed as always, we decided to go to Murrieta's Mexican Restaurant for the dinner. I haven't been here in a long while, but, as I remembered 5 years ago, the food was really good and everyone had enjoyed their meal. Now it's 2016 and the restaurant area and the cantina area were also filled with regulars, watching the game or just having a relaxing time together. As for our service, the young waiter had 5 tables that he was trying his best to serve. But with all the big tables of people he was serving, it caused him to get overloaded and caused many tables to get their food, a few minutes longer then if he only had only 3 big tables. But getting back to the food, it was as good as I remembered it. I had the Albondigas soup, which was very good. Only complaint on that is, you get 2 meatballs in your bowl and the charge is 10 dollars! So it's pretty pricey then it used to be. I also had their Chile Colorado, again also very good in taste and filling. Only complaint is, 15 dollars for that dish. So if the service matched the priceyness of the plates and soups, then yeah I can see paying top dollar for top service, but the restaurant really needs more waiters or waitresses working that big table area, in order to get those orders out in a timely manner. Other then that, we were filled up and glad the dinners were very good.<//Review>< Pictures>
None<//Pictures>

<text>Very disappointed. Been to this place 3 times. First time my friend took me the service was bad, but the food was okay. So, I decided to introduce my husband to this place since it was really close to our house. My husband is very picky and is one of those that doesn't really like to try something different.Well, we went one day, he ordered tacos de papas and it came with a small bowl of bean soup. Surprisingly he really liked it! That was the second time I've been to this place. The third time, he was really  looking forward to have tacos de papas and the bean soup again. It really was his favorite. We went and he ordered his favorite. The food came, my husband had a few spoons of the bean soup and took a bite of one of the tacos and he looked at the other taco and saw a hair on the taco. Told the waiter. The waiter didn't even apologize. He just said that he will bring a new plate. Husband was very patient. New plate came, the tacos were different and the  bean soup looked different. Told the waiter and the waiter asked my husband if he would like to order something else. I insisted that that was my husband's favorite. The waiter still didn't apologize to us and didn't make an effort to get my husband his favorite food. So, I ended up sharing what I ordered with my husband. I was really upset and I felt bad that my husband was really looking forward to having some tacos de papas and bean soup and he didn't get it. He was really excited to go back to this place.
